class="flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex flex-grow flex-col max-w-full"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="e8f7decd-7380-4c58-8708-f570d687c8a1" class="min-h-[20px] text-message flex flex-col items-start gap-3 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 overflow-x-auto"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Those are some popular file formats for sure! In addition to JSON, CSV, and XLSX, you might also encounter:</p><ol><li><p><strong>XML (eXtensible Markup Language):</strong> Similar to JSON, it's used for representing structured data, but uses tags instead of key-value pairs.</p></li><li><p><strong>TXT (Plain Text):</strong> Simple text files with no formatting, often used for configuration files or storing raw text data.</p></li><li><p><strong>HTML (Hypertext Markup Language):</strong> Primarily used for creating web pages, but it's also a structured document format.</p></li><li><p><strong>YAML (YAML Ain't Markup Language):</strong> Human-readable data serialization format, often used for configuration files.</p></li><li><p><strong>SQL (Structured Query Language):</strong> While not a file format per se, SQL scripts are used to interact with relational databases.</p></li><li><p><strong>PDF (Portable Document Format):</strong> Common for sharing documents that need to retain formatting across different platforms.</p></li><li><p><strong>PNG, JPG, GIF (Image Formats):</strong> For storing images, each with its own compression and quality characteristics.</p></li><li><p><strong>MP3, WAV (Audio Formats):</strong> Used for storing audio files, with different compression and quality levels.</p></li><li><p><strong>MP4, AVI, MKV (Video Formats):</strong> For storing video files, each with its own compression and quality features.</p></li><li><p><strong>GIF (Graphics Interchange Format):</strong> Often used for simple animations or short video clips.</p></li></ol><p>These are just a few examples, and there are many more specialized file formats depending on the type of data or content you're dealing with!</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 creating a web API in .NET that processes and validates different file formats is a great project! Here's a simplified outline to get you started:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Create a new ASP.NET Web API Project:</strong>
Open Visual Studio and create a new ASP.NET Web API project.</p></li><li><p><strong>Configure File Upload:</strong>
Enable file upload in your API. You can use the <code>[FromBody]</code> attribute for smaller files like JSON and XML, and for larger files like PDF or XLSX, consider handling them as streams.</p></li><li><p><strong>Add Validation Logic:</strong>
Implement logic to validate each file format. You can use libraries like Json.NET for JSON, System.Xml for XML, and EPPlus for Excel files (XLSX). For PDF, you might want to look into libraries like iTextSharp.</p></li><li><p><strong>Handle CSV Files:</strong>
For CSV, you can use libraries like CsvHelper to parse and validate the data.</p></li><li><p><strong>Define API Endpoints:</strong>
Create specific endpoints for each file type. For example, you might have <code>/api/process/json</code>, <code>/api/process/xml</code>, etc.</p></li><li><p><strong>Exception Handling:</strong>
Implement proper exception handling to provide meaningful error responses when validation fails.</p></li><li><p><strong>Documentation:</strong>

[<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"api/process/json"</span>)</span>]
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IHttpActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJson</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Validate and process JSON data</span>
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Your validation logic here</span>

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Save JSON data to a file on the server</span>
        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> folderPath = <span class="hljs-string">"Path/To/Your/Folder"</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(folderPath, fileName);

        File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData.ToString());

        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
    }
    <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>Make sure to replace <code>"Path/To/Your/Folder"</code> with the actual path to the folder where you want to store the files. class="">using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Web.Http;
using Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
using System.Xml;
using CsvHelper;
using OfficeOpenXml;
using iText.Kernel.Pdf;
using System.Xml.Linq;

namespace fileprocessing.Controllers
{
  

    public class FileProcessingController : ControllerBase
    {
        private const string StorageFolderPath = "Path/To/Your/Folder";

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("api/process/json")]
        public IActionResult ProcessJson([FromBody] JObject jsonData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process JSON data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save JSON data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "json_data.json";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData.ToString());

                return Ok("JSON processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing JSON: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("api/process/xml")]
        public IHttpActionResult ProcessXml([FromBody] XmlDocument xmlData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XML data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XML data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xml_data.xml";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                xmlData.Save(filePath);

                return Ok("XML processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XML: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("api/process/csv")]
        public IHttpActionResult ProcessCsv([FromBody] string csvData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process CSV data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save CSV data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "csv_data.csv";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                File.WriteAllText(filePath, csvData);

                return Ok("CSV processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing CSV: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("api/process/xlsx")]
        public IHttpActionResult ProcessXlsx([FromBody] byte[] xlsxData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XLSX data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XLSX data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xlsx_data.xlsx";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, xlsxData);

                return Ok("XLSX processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XLSX: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("api/process/pdf")]
        public IHttpActionResult ProcessPdf([FromBody] byte[] pdfData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process PDF data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save PDF data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "pdf_data.pdf";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, pdfData);

                return Ok("PDF processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing PDF: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }
    }

data-message-id="aaa2d7c7-79e5-4498-bd27-34471301f7ed" class="min-h-[20px] text-message flex flex-col items-start gap-3 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 overflow-x-auto"><div class="">using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Xml;
using System.Xml.Linq;

namespace fileprocessing.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/process")]
    public class FileProcessingController : ControllerBase
    {
        private const string StorageFolderPath = "Path/To/Your/Folder";

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("jsonfile")]
        public IActionResult ProcessJson([FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process JSON data
                // Your validation logic here

                if (jsonDataFile != null)
                {
                    using (StreamReader reader = new StreamReader(jsonDataFile.OpenReadStream()))
                    {
                        // Read JSON data from the file
                        string jsonData = reader.ReadToEnd();

                        // Save JSON data to a file on the server
                        string fileName = "json_data.json";
                        string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                        System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData);

                        return Ok("JSON processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    return BadRequest("No JSON file provided");
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing JSON: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }


        [HttpPost]
        [Route("jsonbody")]
        public IActionResult ProcessJson([FromBody] JObject jsonData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process JSON data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save JSON data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "json_data.json";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData.ToString());

                return Ok("JSON processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing JSON: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("xml")]
        public IActionResult ProcessXml([FromBody] XmlDocument xmlData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XML data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XML data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xml_data.xml";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                xmlData.Save(filePath);

                return Ok("XML processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XML: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("csv")]
        public IActionResult ProcessCsv([FromBody] string csvData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process CSV data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save CSV data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "csv_data.csv";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, csvData);

                return Ok("CSV processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing CSV: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("xlsx")]
        public IActionResult ProcessXlsx([FromBody] byte[] xlsxData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XLSX data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XLSX data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xlsx_data.xlsx";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, xlsxData);

                return Ok("XLSX processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XLSX: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("pdf")]
        public IActionResult ProcessPdf([FromBody] byte[] pdfData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process PDF data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save PDF data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "pdf_data.pdf";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, pdfData);

                return Ok("PDF processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing PDF: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }
    }
}

dark"><p>Certainly! If you want to read the content of the saved files and print them to the console, you can modify the code as follows:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Xml;

<span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> <span class="hljs-title">fileprocessing.Controllers</span>
{
    [<span class="hljs-meta">ApiController</span>]
    [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"api/process"</span>)</span>]
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span> : <span class="hljs-title">ControllerBase</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> StorageFolderPath = <span class="hljs-string">"Path/To/Your/Folder"</span>;

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Save JSON data to a file on the server</span>
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (StreamReader reader = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> StreamReader(jsonDataFile.OpenReadStream()))
                    {
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Read JSON data from the file</span>
                        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> jsonData = reader.ReadToEnd();

                        System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData);

                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Print file content to console</span>
                        Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content: <span class="hljs-subst">{jsonData}</span>"</span>);

                        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
                    }
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonbody"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonBody</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Save JSON data to a file on the server</span>
                <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
                <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, jsonData.ToString());

                <span class="hljs-comment">// Print file content to console</span>
                Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content: <span class="hljs-subst">{jsonData}</span>"</span>);

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Other methods remain unchanged...</span>

    }
}

if you want to read the file data and convert it to a byte array before printing it to the console, you can modify the code as follows:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Text;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Xml;

<span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> <span class="hljs-title">fileprocessing.Controllers</span>
{
    [<span class="hljs-meta">ApiController</span>]
    [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"api/process"</span>)</span>]
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span> : <span class="hljs-title">ControllerBase</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> StorageFolderPath = <span class="hljs-string">"Path/To/Your/Folder"</span>;

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Save JSON data to a file on the server</span>
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (Stream stream = jsonDataFile.OpenReadStream())
                    {
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Convert file content to byte array</span>
                        <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] fileBytes = ReadFully(stream);

                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Save byte array to a file on the server</span>
                        System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, fileBytes);

                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Print byte array to console</span>
                        Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content as byte array: <span class="hljs-subst">{BitConverter.ToString(fileBytes)}</span>"</span>);

                        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
                    }
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonbody"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonBody</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Convert JSON data to byte array</span>
                <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] jsonDataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jsonData.ToString());

                <span class="hljs-comment">// Save byte array to a file on the server</span>
                <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
                <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, jsonDataBytes);

                <span class="hljs-comment">// Print byte array to console</span>
                Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content as byte array: <span class="hljs-subst">{BitConverter.ToString(jsonDataBytes)}</span>"</span>);

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Other methods remain unchanged...</span>

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Helper method to convert stream to byte array</span>
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] <span class="hljs-title">ReadFully</span>(<span class="hljs-params">Stream input</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (MemoryStream ms = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> MemoryStream())
            {
                input.CopyTo(ms);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ms.ToArray();
            }
        }
    }
}

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Save JSON data to a file on the server</span>
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (Stream stream = jsonDataFile.OpenReadStream())
                    {
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Convert file content to byte array</span>
                        <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] fileBytes = ReadFully(stream);

                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Save byte array to a file on the server</span>
                        System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, fileBytes);

                        <span class="hljs-comment">// Print byte array to console</span>
                        Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content as byte array: <span class="hljs-subst">{BitConverter.ToString(fileBytes)}</span>"</span>);

                        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully. File saved at: "</span> + filePath);
                    }
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] <span class="hljs-title">ReadFully</span>(<span class="hljs-params">Stream input</span>)</span>

class="flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex flex-grow flex-col max-w-full"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="3ebf21f9-6311-4731-8c55-2fc299707c12" class="min-h-[20px] text-message flex flex-col items-start gap-3 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 overflow-x-auto"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Certainly! Clean code emphasizes readability, simplicity, and maintainability. Here are some suggestions to make the code cleaner:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Separate Concerns:</strong></p><ul><li>Consider separating the file processing logic into a service or manager class to adhere to the Single Responsibility Principle.</li><li>Define methods for specific tasks, making each method responsible for one thing.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Use Dependency Injection:</strong></p><ul><li>Inject dependencies like file storage paths or any external services instead of hardcoding them. This improves testability and flexibility.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Handle Edge Cases:</strong></p><ul><li>Add proper error handling for file processing errors, and return meaningful error responses.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Logging:</strong></p><ul><li>Use a logging framework to log errors or relevant information instead of printing to the console.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Consistent Naming:</strong></p><ul><li>Use consistent and meaningful names for methods, variables, and parameters to enhance code readability.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Comments:</strong></p><ul><li>Add comments for complex logic or non-trivial operations to explain the purpose and functioning of the code.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Model Validation:</strong></p><ul><li>Implement model validation for incoming data to ensure that the expected data is being received.</li></ul></li></ol><p>Here's an example of how you can improve the code:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Text;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Xml;

<span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> <span class="hljs-title">fileprocessing.Controllers</span>
{
    [<span class="hljs-meta">ApiController</span>]
    [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"api/process"</span>)</span>]
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span> : <span class="hljs-title">ControllerBase</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span> IFileProcessorService _fileProcessorService;

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFileProcessorService fileProcessorService</span>)</span>
        {
            _fileProcessorService = fileProcessorService;
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] fileBytes = _fileProcessorService.ReadFileAsByteArray(jsonDataFile);

                    _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(fileBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                    _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(fileBytes);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonbody"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonBody</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] jsonDataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jsonData.ToString());

                _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(jsonDataBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(jsonDataBytes);

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Other methods remain unchanged...</span>
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title">IFileProcessorService</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] <span class="hljs-title">ReadFileAsByteArray</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFormFile file</span>)</span>;
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">SaveFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data, <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName</span>)</span>;
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">PrintByteArrayToConsole</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data</span>)</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessorService</span> : <span class="hljs-title">IFileProcessorService</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> StorageFolderPath = <span class="hljs-string">"Path/To/Your/Folder"</span>;

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] <span class="hljs-title">ReadFileAsByteArray</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFormFile file</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (Stream stream = file.OpenReadStream())
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (MemoryStream memoryStream = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> MemoryStream())
                {
                    stream.CopyTo(memoryStream);
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> memoryStream.ToArray();
                }
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">SaveFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data, <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);
            System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, data);
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">PrintByteArrayToConsole</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data</span>)</span>
        {
            Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content as byte array: <span class="hljs-subst">{BitConverter.ToString(data)}</span>"</span>);
        }
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>In this example:</p><ul><li>File processing logic is moved to a <code>FileProcessorService</code> class.</li><li>The controller methods are cleaner and delegate tasks to the service.</li><li>Dependency injection is used to inject the service into the controller.</li><li>Edge cases, such as handling null files, are addressed more explicitly.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 empty:hidden"><div class="text-gray-400 flex self-end lg:self-center justify-center lg:justify-start mt-0 gap-1 visible"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-md p-1 pl-0 text-xs hover:text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-200 disabled:dark:hover:text-gray-400 md:invisible class="">using fileprocessing.ServiceInterface;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Text;
using System.Xml;

namespace fileprocessing.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/process")]
    public class FileProcessingController : ControllerBase
    {
        private const string StorageFolderPath = "Path/To/Your/Folder";
        private readonly IFileProcessorService _fileProcessorService;

        public FileProcessingController(IFileProcessorService fileProcessorService)
        {
            _fileProcessorService = fileProcessorService;
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("jsonfile")]
        public IActionResult ProcessJsonFile([FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile)
        {
            try
            {
                if (jsonDataFile != null)
                {
                    // Save JSON data to a file on the server
                    string fileName = "json_data.json";
                    string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                    using (Stream stream = jsonDataFile.OpenReadStream())
                    {
                        // Convert file content to byte array
                        byte[] fileBytes = ReadFully(stream);

                        // Save byte array to a file on the server
                        System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, fileBytes);

                        // Print byte array to console
                        Console.WriteLine($"File content as byte array: {BitConverter.ToString(fileBytes)}");

                        return Ok("JSON processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    return BadRequest("No JSON file provided");
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing JSON file: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("jsonbody")]
        public IActionResult ProcessJsonBody([FromBody] JObject jsonData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Convert JSON data to byte array
                byte[] jsonDataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jsonData.ToString());

                // Save byte array to a file on the server
                string fileName = "json_data.json";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, jsonDataBytes);

                // Print byte array to console
                Console.WriteLine($"File content as byte array: {BitConverter.ToString(jsonDataBytes)}");

                return Ok("JSON processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing JSON: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("xml")]
        public IActionResult ProcessXml([FromBody] XmlDocument xmlData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XML data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XML data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xml_data.xml";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                xmlData.Save(filePath);

                return Ok("XML processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XML: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("csv")]
        public IActionResult ProcessCsv([FromBody] string csvData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process CSV data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save CSV data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "csv_data.csv";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, csvData);

                // Print CSV data to console
                Console.WriteLine($"CSV data: {csvData}");

                return Ok("CSV processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing CSV: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("xlsx")]
        public IActionResult ProcessXlsx([FromBody] byte[] xlsxData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process XLSX data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save XLSX data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "xlsx_data.xlsx";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, xlsxData);

                // Print byte array to console
                Console.WriteLine($"XLSX data as byte array: {BitConverter.ToString(xlsxData)}");

                return Ok("XLSX processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing XLSX: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        [HttpPost]
        [Route("pdf")]
        public IActionResult ProcessPdf([FromBody] byte[] pdfData)
        {
            try
            {
                // Validate and process PDF data
                // Your validation logic here

                // Save PDF data to a file on the server
                string fileName = "pdf_data.pdf";
                string filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);

                System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, pdfData);

                // Print byte array to console
                Console.WriteLine($"PDF data as byte array: {BitConverter.ToString(pdfData)}");

                return Ok("PDF processed successfully. File saved at: " + filePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return BadRequest($"Error processing PDF: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        // Helper method to convert stream to byte array
        private byte[] ReadFully(Stream input)
        {
            using (MemoryStream ms = new MemoryStream())
            {
                input.CopyTo(ms);
                return ms.ToArray();
            }
        }
    }
}

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span> : <span class="hljs-title">ControllerBase</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span> IFileProcessorService _fileProcessorService;

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFileProcessorService fileProcessorService</span>)</span>
        {
            _fileProcessorService = fileProcessorService;
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] fileBytes = _fileProcessorService.ReadFileAsByteArray(jsonDataFile);

                    _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(fileBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                    _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(fileBytes);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonbody"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonBody</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] jsonDataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jsonData.ToString());

                _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(jsonDataBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(jsonDataBytes);

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Other methods remain unchanged...</span>
    }
}

Note that this code assumes the existence of the <code>IFileProcessorService</code> interface and its implementation in the <code>fileprocessing.ServiceInterface</code> namespace.</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Text;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> fileprocessing.ServiceInterface;

<span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> <span class="hljs-title">fileprocessing.Controllers</span>
{
    [<span class="hljs-meta">ApiController</span>]
    [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"api/process"</span>)</span>]
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span> : <span class="hljs-title">ControllerBase</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span> IFileProcessorService _fileProcessorService;

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessingController</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFileProcessorService fileProcessorService</span>)</span>
        {
            _fileProcessorService = fileProcessorService;
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonfile"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromForm] IFormFile jsonDataFile</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (jsonDataFile != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] fileBytes = _fileProcessorService.ReadFileAsByteArray(jsonDataFile);

                    _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(fileBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                    _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(fileBytes);

                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
                {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">"No JSON file provided"</span>);
                }
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON file: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"jsonbody"</span>)</span>]
        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> IActionResult <span class="hljs-title">ProcessJsonBody</span>(<span class="hljs-params">[FromBody] JObject jsonData</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>
            {
                <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] jsonDataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jsonData.ToString());

                _fileProcessorService.SaveFile(jsonDataBytes, <span class="hljs-string">"json_data.json"</span>);

                _fileProcessorService.PrintByteArrayToConsole(jsonDataBytes);

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> Ok(<span class="hljs-string">"JSON processed successfully."</span>);
            }
            <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception ex)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing JSON: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);
            }
        }

        [<span class="hljs-meta">HttpPost</span>]
        [<span class="hljs-meta">Route(<span class="hljs-string">"xml"</span>)</span>]

        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>

                <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> BadRequest(<span class="hljs-string">$"Error processing XML: <span class="hljs-subst">{ex.Message}</span>"</span>);

If you haven't done that yet, you can create an interface and a service class like this:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">namespace</span> <span class="hljs-title">fileprocessing.ServiceInterface</span>

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">FileProcessorService</span> : <span class="hljs-title">IFileProcessorService</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> StorageFolderPath = <span class="hljs-string">"Path/To/Your/Folder"</span>;

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] <span class="hljs-title">ReadFileAsByteArray</span>(<span class="hljs-params">IFormFile file</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (Stream stream = file.OpenReadStream())
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (MemoryStream memoryStream = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> MemoryStream())
                {
                    stream.CopyTo(memoryStream);
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> memoryStream.ToArray();
                }
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">SaveFile</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data, <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName</span>)</span>
        {
            <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);
            System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, data);
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">PrintByteArrayToConsole</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] data</span>)</span>
        {
            Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"File content as byte array: <span class="hljs-subst">{BitConverter.ToString(data)}</span>"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessXml</span>(<span class="hljs-params">XmlDocument xmlData</span>)</span>
        {

            <span class="hljs-comment">// Your validation and saving logic here</span>

            <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);
            xmlData.Save(filePath);
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessCsv</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> csvData</span>)</span>

            <span class="hljs-comment">// Your validation and saving logic here</span>
            <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> fileName = <span class="hljs-string">"csv_data.csv"</span>;
            <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = Path.Combine(StorageFolderPath, fileName);
            System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filePath, csvData);
        }

            System.IO.File.WriteAllBytes(filePath, xlsxData);
        }

        <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessPdf</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span>[] pdfData</span>)</span>

</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Sample code to iterate over columns:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> OfficeOpenXml;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">ExcelProcessor</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessExcel</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath</span>)</span>
    {
        FileInfo file = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> FileInfo(filePath);

        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (ExcelPackage package = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> ExcelPackage(file))
        {
            ExcelWorksheet worksheet = package.Workbook.Worksheets[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>];

            <span class="hljs-comment">// Assuming the data starts from the second row</span>
            <span class="hljs-built_in">int</span> rowCount = worksheet.Dimension.Rows;
            <span class="hljs-built_in">int</span> colCount = worksheet.Dimension.Columns;

            <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">int</span> col = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>; col &lt;= colCount; col++)
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">int</span> row = <span class="hljs-number">2</span>; row &lt;= rowCount; row++)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access cell value</span>
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> cellValue = worksheet.Cells[row, col].Value;

                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Process the cell value as needed</span>
                    Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"Column: <span class="hljs-subst">{col}</span>, Row: <span class="hljs-subst">{row}</span>, Value: <span class="hljs-subst">{cellValue}</span>"</span>);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><h3>Iterating Over Columns in CSV using CsvHelper:</h3><ol><li><p>Install the CsvHelper NuGet package:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>bash</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">Install-Package CsvHelper
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Sample code to iterate over columns:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> CsvHelper;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> CsvHelper.Configuration;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.Globalization;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">CsvProcessor</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessCsv</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath</span>)</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> reader = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> StreamReader(filePath))
        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> csv = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> CsvReader(reader, <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> CsvConfiguration(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)))
        {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// Read the header row</span>
            csv.Read();
            csv.ReadHeader();

            <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (csv.Read())
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">foreach</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> header <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> csv.Context.HeaderRecord)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access cell value</span>
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> cellValue = csv.GetField(header);

                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Process the cell value as needed</span>
                    Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"Column: <span class="hljs-subst">{header}</span>, Value: <span class="hljs-subst">{cellValue}</span>"</span>);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><p>Make sure to adjust the code based on your specific requirements and file structures. <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">CsvProcessor</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">ProcessCsv</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath</span>)</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> reader = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> StreamReader(filePath))
        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> csv = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> CsvReader(reader, <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> CsvConfiguration(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)))
        {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// Read the header row</span>
            csv.ReadHeader();

            <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (csv.Read())
            {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">record</span> = csv.GetRecord&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">dynamic</span>&gt;(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Using dynamic to access fields by name</span>

                <span class="hljs-keyword">foreach</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> field <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">record</span>)
                {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access cell value</span>
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> cellValue = field.Value;

                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Process the cell value as needed</span>
                    Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"Column: <span class="hljs-subst">{field.Key}</span>, Value: <span class="hljs-subst">{cellValue}</span>"</span>);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>In this updated code:</p><ul><li>The <code>ReadHeader</code> method is used to read the header row.</li><li><code>csv.GetRecord&lt;dynamic&gt;()</code> is used to read the record dynamically, allowing you to access fields by name.</li></ul><p>Make sure you have the latest version of CsvHelper installed. To create a PDF file in C#, you can use a library like iTextSharp. iTextSharp is a popular library for working with PDF documents. Below is a simple class that demonstrates how to create a PDF file using iTextSharp:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp"><span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> System.IO;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> iText.Kernel.Pdf;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> iText.Layout;
<span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> iText.Layout.Element;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">PdfCreator</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">CreatePdf</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath, <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> content</span>)</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Create a PdfWriter object to write to the specified file path</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> writer = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> PdfWriter(filePath))
        {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// Create a PdfDocument object</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> pdf = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> PdfDocument(writer))
            {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Create a Document object to add elements to the PDF</span>
                <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> document = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Document(pdf);

                <span class="hljs-comment">// Add content to the PDF</span>
                document.Add(<span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Paragraph(content));

                <span class="hljs-comment">// The document is automatically closed and saved when exiting the using block</span>
            }
        }
    }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">Program</span>
{
    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">Main</span>()</span>
    {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Example usage</span>
        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> filePath = <span class="hljs-string">"example.pdf"</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> content = <span class="hljs-string">"Hello, this is a sample PDF content."</span>;

        PdfCreator pdfCreator = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> PdfCreator();
        pdfCreator.CreatePdf(filePath, content);

        Console.WriteLine(<span class="hljs-string">$"PDF created successfully at: <span class="hljs-subst">{Path.GetFullPath(filePath)}</span>"</span>);
    }
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>Make sure to install the iTextSharp library using the NuGet Package Manager Console:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>bash</span><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">Install-Package itext7
</code></div></div></pre><p>In the above class:</p><ul><li>The <code>PdfWriter</code> is used to create a PDF file at the specified file path.</li><li>The <code>PdfDocument</code> represents the PDF
